. 
. *define program to export direct, indirect and total effects
. capture program drop te_direct

. program te_direct, eclass
  1.     quietly estat teffects
  2.     mat b = r(direct)
  3.     mat V = r(V_direct)
  4.     local N = e(N)
  5.     ereturn post b V, obs(`N')
  6.     ereturn local cmd te_direct 
  7. end

. 
. capture program drop te_indirect

. program te_indirect, eclass
  1.     quietly estat teffects
  2.     mat b = r(indirect)
  3.     mat V = r(V_indirect)
  4.     ereturn post b V
  5.     ereturn local cmd te_indirect 
  6. end

. 
. capture program drop te_total

. program te_total, eclass
  1.     quietly estat teffects
  2.     mat b = r(total)
  3.     mat V = r(V_total)
  4.     ereturn post b V
  5.     ereturn local cmd te_total 
  6. end

. 
.
